[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8Parser.handleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:170[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8Parser._parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:92[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.M3U8ParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:39[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: b782adc79e9c6729[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA medium-severity Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was detected during [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing. The fuzzer attempted to open a socket connection to “jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m” while [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing a potentially untrusted playlist. The built-in SSRF sanitizer in Jazzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflagged this outbound connection attempt as a security issue.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer input triggered the application’s HTTP client code to open a network [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection to an external host [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazzer.com[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m based on data read from an M3U8 [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplaylist. This outbound connection attempt is considered a Server-Side Request [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mForgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m risk because it allows an attacker to coerce the server into [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitiating arbitrary requests to external or internal services.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue has been classified as Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, as indicated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the exception `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServer Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception is thrown by `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` in the Jazzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer library.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The vulnerable call chain originates in the parser for M3U8 playlists [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`M3U8Parser.handleLink` → `URLConnection.getInputStream` → `Socket.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows that the code uses `java.net.HttpURLConnection` to fetch [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote resources referenced by the playlist.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`M3U8ParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply invokes the parser’s `parseOne` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod and is not the root cause; it serves as an entry point for feeding untrusted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • M3U8Parser class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially the `handleLink` and `_parse` methods[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to see how [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURLs are extracted and passed to the HTTP client.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • [0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls in `org.apache.tika.io.TikaInputStream` which [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrigger the HTTP request.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any configuration or custom usage of `java.net.HttpURLConnection` or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.net.Socket` in the parsing flow.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • SSRF detection logic in [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery` to understand [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhat destinations are blocked or allowed.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAttempted connection to: jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m597[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m598[0m[39m:        URLConnection connection = [0m[1;35murl.openConnection[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m599[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m600[0m[39m:        String path = [0m[1;35murl.getPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m601[0m[39m:        int slash = [0m[1;35mpath.lastIndexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m602[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mslash + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m < [0m[1;35mpath.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m works even with [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m![0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m603[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mpath.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[39mslash + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m604[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m605[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the Issue & Root Cause  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The SSRF arises because [0m[1;35mM3U8Parser.handleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m blindly calls  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   for any “http…” URI extracted from the playlist. This opens a real TCP socket to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary hosts—exactly what Jazzer’s SSRF sanitizer flags.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy: Disable Untrusted HTTP Fetch in M3U8Parser.handleLink  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We will remove the automatic [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fetch of remote playlist segments. Instead,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mM3U8Parser will continue to record all links in metadata [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno longer open network connections to HTTP/HTTPS URIs. This anchors SSRF mitigation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely within the parser and avoids touching utility classes or harness code.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In M3U8Parser.handleLink [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m153[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m174[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Retain the call to `[0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` so that the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser still records every URI.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor comment out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m the entire HTTP/HTTPS branch that creates a `new [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and calls `[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After adding `PLAY_LIST_LINK`, immediately return unconditionally [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplement a minimal scheme check for local files, if desired[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preventing any [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote fetch.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Example transformed pseudocode:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private void [0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException, SAXException [0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String nextLine = [0m[1;35mgetNextContentLine[0m[1;39m([0m[39mreader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Prevent SSRF: do not fetch external HTTP/HTTPS resources.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove imports of `java.net.URL`, `EmbeddedDocumentExtractor`, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaInputStream`, `BodyContentHandler`, and any other classes used solely for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote fetch.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All playlist URIs still appear in metadata as before.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parsing of local/relative URIs or inline content remains unaffected [0m[1;39m([0m[39msince [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey were never fetched remotely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other parsers or utility classes are modified, thus avoiding unintended [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mside effects.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The remote‐fetch feature was optional; disabling it does not break the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39messential “playlist parsing” functionality and preserves existing tests.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Security Impact  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By eliminating all outbound connections from this code path, SSRF is fully [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigated.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch is minimal and self‐contained; it does not alter any fuzz harness or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcore utility code.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzer runs will no longer attempt to connect to attacker‐controlled hosts, so[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe SSRF sanitizer in Jazzer will not be triggered.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should the project later decide to reintroduce controlled remote fetch, it can[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdo so behind an explicit configuration or whitelist.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side‐Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Loss of embedded segment extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno longer fetching media segments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     *Mitigation*: In practice, downstream consumers of M3U8Parser rarely require [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull segment parsing from remote URIs. If this feature is critical, it can be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreimplemented under a strict allowlist or via an opt‐in ParseContext flag.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unused imports and variables in handleLink will be dead code; a simple cleanup[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass will remove them.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References to Similar Patterns  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other parsers in Tika disable remote fetch by default and require explicit [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., office document parsers may skip external DTD fetch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Disabling remote retrieval in M3U8Parser aligns behavior with “safe by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault” security posture adopted elsewhere in the codebase.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. No Changes to Harness or Tests  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`M3U8ParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains untouched.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing unit tests for M3U8Parser that verify metadata extraction will pass [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new dependencies or external configuration are introduced.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mEmbeddedContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxhtml[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, m,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:                        true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m173[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-audiov[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mideo-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/m3/M3U8Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:163[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m166[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:            return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Analyze the broken patch  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The previous patch removed the HTTP‐fetch block in `handleLink` but [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minadvertently inserted or misaligned braces, leaving method‐body code floating [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside any class/method and triggering “class, interface, enum, or record [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected” compilation errors.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must reapply the SSRF patch against the original code, ensuring that we:  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Replace the HTTP fetch logic with a single `return` immediately after [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecording the link.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Preserve exactly one closing brace for `handleLink` and the existing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass‐closing brace.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Steps to implement the corrected patch  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `M3U8Parser.java` and locate the `handleLink` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m153[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Inside `handleLink`, remove all lines from the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` block through its matching `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39moriginally [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m164[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m174[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Immediately after the `[0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` statement, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsert a single `return;` statement.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure that after this `return`, only one `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` remains to close `handleLink`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDo not add or remove any other braces.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Leave the final brace [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m200[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m untouched to close the `M3U8Parser` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Maintained and altered functionality  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Functionality preserved:  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • All playlist links [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTTP or otherwise[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to be recorded in metadata. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Non-HTTP links exit early exactly as before.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Functionality removed:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No network fetch or embedded parsing is performed on HTTP links, eliminating[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe SSRF vector.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parser stability:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Method and class brace balance is fully restored; no compilation errors [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Tests and harnesses are unaffected.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Meets security requirement: eliminates unvalidated URL fetch.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Restores syntactic correctness: no dangling braces or orphaned code.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns with the original SSRF patch intent while rectifying the accidental [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrace misplacement.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side effect: embedded content from HTTP playlists is no longer parsed inline. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf downstream consumers need this, consider an out-of-band, whitelist-driven [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownload mechanism.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: document the change in release notes and, if necessary, provide [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguidance on secure playlist fetching in a separate module or under strict [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURL‐validation policies.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validation  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn clean compile` to ensure no compilation errors in [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parser-audiovideo-module`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Execute existing unit and integration tests to confirm no regressions.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the Jazzer SSRF fuzzer to verify that the SSRF finding is resolved [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout introducing new issues.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
